***fen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a> (70131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fenne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fenn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a>; marsh; mud; dirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fanją</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fean</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veen.html>veen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fenn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pen-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bog, mire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">enach</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swamp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">pannean</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peat-bog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पङ्क</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paṅka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marsh, mud, mire, slough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of wetland fed by ground water and runoff, containing peat below the waterline, characteristically alkaline.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="w:The Tempest">The Tempest</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act I, scene ii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA4">page 4</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">Caliban</span>: As wicked dewe, as <a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>ere</a> my mother bruſh'd / With Rauens feather from vnwholeſome <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>Fen</a></b> / Drop on you both : A Southweſt blow on <a href = vnd.unilang:yee.html>yee</a>, / And bliſter you all ore.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1807</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Wordsworth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Wordsworth">William Wordsworth</a>, "England, 1802," collected in <i>Poems</i> (1807):
<dl><dd>Milton! thou shouldst be living at this hour:</dd>
<dd>England hath need of <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a>: she <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></b></dd>
<dd>Of stagnant waters <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1842</b>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Author:Henry_Wadsworth_Longfellow" class="extiw" title="s:Author:Henry Wadsworth Longfellow"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Wadsworth Longfellow</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Slave_in_the_Dismal_Swamp" class="extiw" title="s:The Slave in the Dismal Swamp">The Slave in the Dismal Swamp</a></i>, from <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Poems_on_Slavery" class="extiw" title="s:Poems on Slavery">Poems on Slavery</a>:
<dl><dd>In dark <b>fens</b> of the Dismal Swamp / The hunted Negro lay; [...]</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_le_Carr%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John le Carré">John le Carré</a>,  <cite><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Perfect_Spy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Perfect Spy">A <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>Perfect</a> Spy</a></i></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> freezing to death in the <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> mud of the Suffolk <b>fens</b>, too proud to go home without a catch.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">unit</span> of <span class="Latn" lang="en">currency</span> in <span class="Latn" lang="en">China</span>, one-hundredth of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">yuan</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fan</i>, by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></i> as the plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>normally plural</i>, <i>singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">fan</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> fandom <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:fans.html>fans</a>; a plural form used by enthusiasts of science fiction, fantasy, and anime, partly from whimsy and partly to distinguish themselves from <a href = vnd.unilang:fans.html>fans</a> of sport, etc.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1951</b> May 21,  Sargeant, Winthrop,  “Through the Interstellar <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>Looking</a> Glass”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Life_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Life (magazine)">Life</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=fVEEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA127">[1]</a></sup>, volume 30, number 21, page 127:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Sad to relate, some of the European delegates <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> probably insurgents rather than true <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></b>. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> But the Europeans could be counted on to take the long view, and many of them would probably turn out to be real <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></b> and fenne after all.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b> September 3,  lurkertype,  “Worldcon 75 Chair Responds”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File_770" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:File 770">File 770</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://file770.com/?p=30440">[2]</a></sup>, Comments:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">So I’m glad the attached <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a> block <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> entirely reserved for disabled <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fen.html>fen</a></b>! Traveling on mass transit <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> tiring <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> when everything’s up to code.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***fennel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fennel.html>fennel</a> (93557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fenel</i>, from the late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">finuðl</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">finule</i> (weak feminine forms); <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fenol</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">finul</i> (masculine forms), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fenoil</i>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*fēnuclum</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fēnoclum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fēnuculum</i>, from the Classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">faeniculum</i>, a diminutive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">faenum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">finocchio</i>, the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Occitan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Occitan language">Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">fenolh</i>, the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fenouil</i>, and the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">hinojo</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">finocchio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fennel.html>fennel</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fennels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A plant, <i>Foeniculum vulgare</i>, of the parsley family, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a sweet, anise-like flavor.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The bulb, leaves, or stalks of the plant, eaten as a vegetable.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The seeds of the <a href = vnd.unilang:fennel.html>fennel</a> plant used as a spice in cooking.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***fet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fet.html>fet</a> (93553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fetten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">feten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fetian</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fatian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring, fetch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably a conflation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fetaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ped-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk, stumble, fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hold, seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ped-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vatten.html>vatten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to catch, grab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fassen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lay hold of, seize, take, hold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">feta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to find one's way</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fetch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fet.html>fet</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fets</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fetting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:fet.html>fet</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fetch</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***fiddler.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiddler.html>fiddler</a> (18066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fiþelere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fiþelere</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fiþele</i>.  Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fiddle</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiddler.html>fiddler</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fiddlers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who plays the fiddle.</li>
<li>One who fiddles.
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, Yasmin Alibhai-Brown, <i>The drama of my life</i> (in <i>The Independent</i> online, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/theatre-dance/features/the-drama-of-my-life-483792.html">[1]</a>)
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the self-controlled, cautious, nifty <a href = vnd.unilang:merchants.html>merchants</a>, decorous <b>fiddlers</b> of accounts, hoarders of wealth, excellent bribers, family and community <a href = vnd.unilang:creatures.html>creatures</a> governed by manners.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A burrowing crab of the genus <i>Gelasimus</i>, of many species. The male <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> one claw very much enlarged, and often holds it in a position similar to that in which a musician holds a fiddle.</li>
<li>The common European sandpiper (<i>Actitis hypoleucos</i>); so called because it continually oscillates its body.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fiddlist</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fiddleist</span> <i>(dated)</i></li></ul>

<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;"><a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>Terms</a> derived from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:fiddler.html>fiddler</a></i></div>

***fie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fie.html>fie</a> (49567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fi</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Old French and Middle English (with a possible additional influence from Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fie.html>fie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often followed by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">on</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">upon</i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Used to express distaste, disgust, or outrage.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:fie.html>Fie</a></b> upon you, you devilish fool!</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>March 1920</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:alice.html>Alice</a> Ballantine Kirjassoff (quote sourced to <a href = vnd.unilang:kim.html>Kim</a> Soan),  “FORMOSA THE BEAUTIFUL”, in  <cite>National Geographic Magazine</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/nationalgeograp371920nati/page/284">[1]</a></sup>, page 284-5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"I pleaded with my companions to spare his life, and they <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:fie.html>Fie</a></b>! shame upon you! You have a Chinese heart.' Then they <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> upon <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to kill <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> as well, so I withdrew my petition. After that they cut off the woodsman's head, and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> returned home."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***fiend.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a> (131159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">feend</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fēnd</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">feond</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">viend</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">veond</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enemy; <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fēond</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enemy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fijandz</i>. (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fjándi</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">fjandi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">fjende</i>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">fiende</i>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">fiende</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fijân</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Feend</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>Fiend</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Feind</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐌹𐌾𐌰𐌽𐌳𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fijands</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), with all of them meaning <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">foe</i>. The Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> and Gothic <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> are present participles of the corresponding verbs <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fjá</i>/<i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐌹𐌾𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fijan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पीयति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pī́yati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(he) reviles</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fiends</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A devil or <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a>; a malignant or diabolical being; an evil spirit.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1845</b>, E.A. Poe, "The Raven"
<dl><dd>"Be that word our sign of parting, bird or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a>!</b>"</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A very evil person.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An enemy; a foe.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Religion teaches us to love everybody, be one <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></b> or friend.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religious<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The enemy of mankind, specifically, the Devil; <a href = vnd.unilang:satan.html>Satan</a>.
<ul><li><b>1971</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keith_Thomas_(historian)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Keith Thomas (historian)">Keith Thomas</a>, <i>Religion and the Decline of Magic</i>, Folio Society 2012, p. 35:
<dl><dd>At the confirmation ceremony the bishop would lay his hands on the child and tie around its forehead a linen <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> believed to strengthen him against the assaults of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></b> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An addict or fanatic.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He's <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> a jazz <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></b> since his teenage years.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dope.html>dope</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></b></i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiets.html>fiets</a> (2633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Various <a href = vnd.unilang:hypotheses.html>hypotheses</a> exist: from the dialectal verb <i>vietse</i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:fietsen.html>fietsen</a></i> (“to move quickly”), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vite</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Less likely <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a corruption of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vélocipède</i>, <i>fieselepee</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fietsen.html>fietsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ride or cycle a bicycle, to bike</li></ol>

<li>fine, thin</li>
<li>delicate, meticulous</li></ol>

***fijnproever.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fijnproever.html>fijnproever</a> (51961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fijn.html>fijn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:proeven.html>proeven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, likely a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Feinschmecker</i>. Older Dutch also used the phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fijne.html>fijne</a> proever</i> in the same meaning.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fijnproever.html>fijnproever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fijnproevers.html>fijnproevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fijnproever.html>fijnproevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">fijnproefster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A food connoisseur, a gourmet <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who appreciate quality food</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>. <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1736</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> weereldt in <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> verscheidentheidt; Of <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> mannelyk <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> ontbyt, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Jufferlijk <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a></i>, publ. by Jacobus Loveringh, page 242.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>Zie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Wyn veroordeeldt, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> wagten <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vermaak.html>vermaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zinnelykheid <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <b>Fynproever</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:behaagt.html>behaagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> toeſtaan.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">See the wine be condemned there, and one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to wait with drinking with pleasure until it pleases the temperament of the <b>connoisseur</b> to be willing to allow it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1835</b> July 28, Ch., "<a href = vnd.unilang:oproerig.html>Oproerig</a> berigt <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kok.html>kok</a>", <i>Leeuwarder <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, No. 69, page 3.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorst.html>Vorst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> vraat, <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekkerbek.html>lekkerbek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fijnproever.html>fijnproever</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fatsoenlijk.html>fatsoenlijk</a> spijzer.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Monarch <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a glutton, not a gourmand, not a <b>connoisseur</b>, not <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> a refined eater.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A connoisseur <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one with a refined taste</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>. <span class="defdate">[from mid 19th c.]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fik.html>fik</a> (6515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fix</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixen</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fastened; fixed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīxus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">immovable; steady; stable; fixed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīgere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drive in; stick; fasten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeygʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to jab; ***filosoof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:filosoof.html>filosoof</a> (11263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:filosofe.html>filosofe</a></i>, possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">philosophe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">philosophus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φῐλόσοφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">philósophos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
